<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слипаться.html>слипа́ться</a> (16269)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слипаться.html>слипа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slipátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слипнуться.html>сли́пнуться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick together, to stick to each other</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:слипаться.html>слипа́ться</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:слипнуться.html>сли́пнуться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-лип-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***слипнуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слипнуться.html>сли́пнуться</a> (13661)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:липнуть.html>ли́пнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lípnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слипнуться.html>сли́пнуться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slípnutʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слипаться.html>слипа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick together, to stick to each other</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>сли́п<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нуть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3°a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:слипаться.html>слипа́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-лип-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ну</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слиться.html>сли́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сливаться.html>слива́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flow together, to interflow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to merge, to fuse, to blend</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слить.html>слить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слива.html>слив</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sliv</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">слива́ние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">slivánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

</p>
<ol><li>too (more than enough), too much

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:словеса.html>словеса́</a> (28924)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Archaic plural of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slóvo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">word</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (originally an <i>s</i>-stem).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:словеса.html>словеса́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slovesá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:словеса.html>слове́с</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ironic or literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> words, text, verbiage</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:словечко.html>слове́чко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slovéčko</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:словечко.html>слове́чка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:словечко.html>слове́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:словечко.html>слове́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slóvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: word</li></ol>

***словно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a> (260)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slóvno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>like, as if
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>дере́вья</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крепкий.html>кре́пкие</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a></b> сама́ны, <a href = vnd.unilang:затвердевший.html>затверде́вшие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:горячий.html>горя́чим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:солнце.html>со́лнцем</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Derévʹja krépkije, <b>slóvno</b> samány, zatverdévšije pod gorjáčim sólncem.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The trees are sturdy, <b>like</b> adobe bricks hardened under the hot sun.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>as it were
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бо</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бело́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́ло</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пурга.html>пурге́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nébo býlo beló/bélo, <b>slóvno</b> v purgé.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The sky was white, <b>as it were</b> in a snowstorm.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slóvno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>it seems (that), it looks like <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">for expressing conditional, imaginary, or apparent things or action</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́дел</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:единорог.html>единоро́га</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бе</a>.</i></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><i>Ja <b>slóvno</b> vídel jedinoróga, kotóryj letál na nébe.</i></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><i><b>It looked like</b> to me that I was seeing a unicorn that was flying in the sky.</i></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li>The meaning of <b><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">by</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b> is already implied. Hence <b><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slóvno by</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b> is the same as <b><a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a></b>.</li>
<li>Due to the <i>invisible</i> <b><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">by</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b> in the conjunction and particle <b><a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a></b>, any finite verb governed by either of these usages must be in the past tense.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">as if, as it were</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:будто.html>бу́дто</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">búdto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:будто.html>бу́дто</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kak búdto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точно.html>то́чно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tóčno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">it seems (that)</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>ка́жется</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kážetsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>кажи́сь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kažísʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:никак.html>ника́к</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nikák</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***слово.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> (104)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*slȍvo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">word</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱléwos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fame</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slóvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>word, term
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грубый.html>гру́бое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">grúboje <b>slóvo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">harsh <b>word</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устаревший.html>устаре́вшее</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ustarévšeje <b>slóvo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">obsolete <b>word</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>speech, address</li>
<li>promise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушать.html>наруша́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">narušátʹ <b>slóvo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break one's word, to go back upon / on one's word (breaking promise or contract)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>сло́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1c  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка). <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сочетание.html>сочета́ниях</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>ти́па</a> «<i><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i>», «<i><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i>», «<i><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́ву</a></i>» <a href = vnd.unilang:ударение.html>ударе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:падать.html>па́дать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>предло́г</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> «<i><a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i>» <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:превращаться.html>превраща́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> клитику.

***слог.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слог.html>слог</a> (10186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сълогъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭlogŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + the root of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слог.html>слог</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slog</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слог.html>сло́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слог.html>сло́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слог.html>слого́в</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">слогово́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">phonology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> syllable</li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сложить.html>сложи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">složítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:складывать.html>скла́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lay together, to put together, to pile up, to heap, to stack</li>
<li>to pack up</li>
<li>to add, to sum up</li>
<li>to make, to assemble, to put together</li>
<li><i>song, rhyme</i> to compose, to make up</li>
<li>to fold</li></ol>

***сложиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сложиться.html>сложи́ться</a> (2420)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сложить.html>сложи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">složítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сложиться.html>сложи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">složítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:складываться.html>скла́дываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to chip in; to club together (with), to pool (with), to pool one's money / resources</li>
<li>to (be) form(ed), to develop, to turn out, to take shape; to arise <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a situation, relationship</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сложиться.html>сложи́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:основной.html>основны́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:факт.html>фа́ктов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́лу</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>složílasʹ</b> kartína osnovnýx fáktov po étomu délu.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have a grip of the essential facts of this case.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">A picture of core facts about this case <b>took shape</b> for me.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опасный.html>опа́сная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ситуация.html>ситуа́ция</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сложиться.html>сложи́лась</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Opásnaja situácija <b>složílasʹ</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">A dangerous situation took shape.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сложить.html>сложи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">složítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>сло<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жи́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:складываться.html>скла́дываться</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сложный.html>сло́жный</a> (1313)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">слож(и́ть)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slož(ítʹ)</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pile up; to fold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сложный.html>сло́жный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slóžnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сложне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сложне́й</b>)

<li>complicated, intricate</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сломать.html>слома́ть</a> (2832)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломать.html>лома́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lomátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сломать.html>слома́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slomátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломать.html>лома́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to break, to fracture
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сломать.html>слома́ешь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jazýk <b>slomáješʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it's a real tongue-twister</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">you will break (my) tongue</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to demolish, to pull down (a house)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to destroy, to break down, to ruin</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сломаться.html>слома́ться</a> (8194)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сломать.html>слома́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slomátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сломаться.html>слома́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slomátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломаться.html>лома́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break, to break up, to fracture, to split</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break down (of a device, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to collapse, to fall apart</li>
<li>to crack, to break (of the voice)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сломать.html>слома́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slomátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>сло<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>ма́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:ломаться.html>лома́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-лом-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сломить.html>сломи́ть</a> (10435)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломить.html>ломи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lomítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сломить.html>сломи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slomítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to break, to crush
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сломить.html>сломи́ть</a></b> чьё-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:упорство.html>упо́рство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>slomítʹ</b> čʹjó-libo upórstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to subdue/crush someone's obstinacy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сломить.html>сломи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сопротивление.html>сопротивле́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:враг.html>врага́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>slomítʹ</b> soprotivlénije vragá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break down the enemy's resistance</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>A present adverbial participle <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сломя.html>сломя́</a></span> appears in the expression <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сломя.html>сломя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́лову</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slomjá gólovu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (see derived terms below).</li></ul>
